| [test\_memory\_corruption](https://github.com/lumc01/Lumvorax/blob/main/test_memory_corruption "test_memory_corruption") | [test\_memory\_corruption](https://github.com/lumc01/Lumvorax/blob/main/test_memory_corruption "test_memory_corruption") | [Improve memory safety and stability of core operations](https://github.com/lumc01/Lumvorax/commit/c2b06487c6e07aebf91e8d57f0b09795966a5fab "Improve memory safety and stability of core operations  This commit introduces several enhancements to memory management and error handling within the LUM core and VORAX operations. Key changes include:  - **`lum_safe_destroy` Enhancement**:   - Implemented protection against double-freeing of LUM objects by adding a `DESTROYED_MAGIC` check.   - Added checks for memory corruption by verifying `memory_address` consistency, preventing direct freeing of LUMs that might be part of a group or have been copied.   - Modified the function to mark LUMs as destroyed and invalidate pointers even when not freeing memory, ensuring pointer safety.  - **`lum_group_destroy` Robustness**:   - Introduced comprehensive validation for group integrity, including checks for `count` vs. `capacity` and suspicious large values for both.   - If corruption is detected, the group structure is zeroed out to prevent further memory access errors.   - Added an extra validation step for the `lums` pointer to prevent freeing clearly corrupted or invalid addresses.   - Corrected a scenario where `group->lums` was incorrectly pointing to the group itself, preventing a potential double-free or invalid free.  - **Demonstration Updates (`main.c`)**:   - Clarified the ownership transfer in `demo_basic_lum_operations` by commenting that `lum_group_add` copies LUMs and the originals remain under the caller's ownership.   - Modified the cleanup in `demo_basic_lum_operations` to use `lum_safe_destroy` for the original LUMs, aligning with the new safe destruction logic.   - Refactored `demo_vorax_operations` to use safer group creation and destruction patterns, and corrected the VORAX fuse operation to use `result_group` instead of `output_group`.  - **`vorax_move` Logic**:   - Modified the LUM removal logic in `vorax_move` to use a per-group count (`moved_from_this_group`) to accurately reduce `source_group->count`, preventing potential underflow or incorrect count reductions.  - **New Test Files**:   - Added `test_memory_corruption.c` to specifically test the memory safety improvements, including double destruction, group/individual LUM lifecycles, and multiple group destructions.   - Added `test_parser_corruption.c` to test the VORAX parser's robustness and memory handling during parsing and execution, ensuring proper cleanup of AST and execution contexts.  These changes significantly enhance the reliability and safety of memory management within the project, reducing the risk of crashes due to double-frees, memory corruption, or invalid memory access. ## Repository files navigation

# LUM/VORAX System - Version V32 (Advanced Optimization)

[Permalink: LUM/VORAX System - Version V32 (Advanced Optimization)](https://github.com/lumc01/Lumvorax#lumvorax-system---version-v32-advanced-optimization)

## Présentation

[Permalink: Présentation](https://github.com/lumc01/Lumvorax#pr%C3%A9sentation)

LUM/VORAX est un moteur de calcul haute performance écrit en C, conçu pour les environnements temps-réel exigeants. La version V32 apporte des optimisations de pointe au niveau kernel-space (slab allocation, lock-free, async I/O).

## Nouvelles Fonctionnalités V32

[Permalink: Nouvelles Fonctionnalités V32](https://github.com/lumc01/Lumvorax#nouvelles-fonctionnalit%C3%A9s-v32)

- **Moteur d'Optimisation Massif :** SIMD AVX2, Slab Allocator, Async Logging.
- **Architecture Distribuée :** Support multi-noeuds (Cluster Ready).
- **Sécurité Critique :** Audit hardening et monitoring temps-réel.
- **Export WASM :** Prêt pour le déploiement WebAssembly.

## Installation & Compilation

[Permalink: Installation & Compilation](https://github.com/lumc01/Lumvorax#installation--compilation)

```
make all        # Compilation optimisée
gcc -O3 -march=native -mavx2 -I src src/tests/test_unit_v32_all_modules.c ... -o v32_test -lpthread -lm
./v32_test      # Exécution de la suite de tests complète (14 modules)
```

## Structure du Projet

[Permalink: Structure du Projet](https://github.com/lumc01/Lumvorax#structure-du-projet)

- `src/optimization/` : Cœur des performances (Async Log, Slab, SIMD, Lock-free, LZ4, MMap).
- `src/security/` : Audit et Hardening.
- `src/monitoring/` : Alerting système.
- `src/distributed/` : Réseau et Cluster.
- `src/wasm/` : Exportation WebAssembly.

## Rapports de Performance

[Permalink: Rapports de Performance](https://github.com/lumc01/Lumvorax#rapports-de-performance)

Consultez `reports/FINAL_VALIDATION_REPORT_V32.md` pour les métriques détaillées.
